  <th data-stat="player" align="left"  class="tooltip sort_default_asc show_partial_when_sorting"  tip="<strong>Player Name</strong><br><strong>Bold</strong> can mean player is active for this team<br>or player has appeared in MLB<br>* means LHP or LHB,<br># means switch hitter,<br>+ can mean HOFer.">Batting</th>
  <th data-stat="AB" align="center"  class="tooltip"  tip="At Bats" data-filter="1" data-name="At Bats">AB</th>
  <th data-stat="R" align="center"  class="tooltip"  tip="Runs Scored/Allowed" data-filter="1" data-name="Runs Scored">R</th>
  <th data-stat="H" align="center"  class="tooltip"  tip="Hits/Hits Allowed" data-filter="1" data-name="Hits">H</th>
  <th data-stat="RBI" align="center"  class="tooltip"  tip="Runs Batted In" data-filter="1" data-name="Runs Batted In">RBI</th>
  <th data-stat="BB" align="center"  class="tooltip"  tip="Bases on Balls/Walks" data-filter="1" data-name="Bases on Balls">BB</th>
  <th data-stat="SO" align="center"  class="tooltip"  tip="Strikeouts" data-filter="1" data-name="Strikeouts">SO</th>
  <th data-stat="PA" align="center"  class="tooltip"  tip="<strong>Plate Appearances</strong><br>When available, we use actual plate appearances from play-by-play game accounts<br>Otherwise estimated using AB + BB + HBP + SF + SH,<br>which excludes catcher interferences.<br>When <span class=tooltip>this color</span> click for a summary of each PA." data-filter="1" data-name="Plate Appearances">PA</th>
  <th data-stat="batting_avg" align="center"  class="tooltip hide_non_quals"  tip="<strong>Hits/At Bats</strong><br>For recent years, leaders need 3.1 PA<br>per team game played<br>Bold indicates highest BA using current stats<br><span class=glimmer>Gold</span> means awarded title at end of year." data-filter="1" data-name="Batting Average">BA</th>
  <th data-stat="onbase_perc" align="center"  class="tooltip hide_non_quals"  tip="<strong>(H + BB + HBP)/(At Bats + BB + HBP + SF)</strong><br>For recent years, leaders need 3.1 PA<br>per team game played" data-filter="1" data-name="On-Base%">OBP</th>
  <th data-stat="slugging_perc" align="center"  class="tooltip hide_non_quals"  tip="<strong>Total Bases/At Bats or <br>(1B + 2*2B + 3*3B + 4*HR)/AB</strong><br>For recent years, leaders need 3.1 PA<br>per team game played" data-filter="1" data-name="Slugging %">SLG</th>
  <th data-stat="onbase_plus_slugging" align="center"  class="tooltip hide_non_quals"  tip="<strong>On-Base + Slugging Percentages </strong><br>For recent years, leaders need 3.1 PA<br>per team game played" data-filter="1" data-name="On-Base Plus Slugging">OPS</th>
  <th data-stat="pitches" align="center"  class="tooltip"  tip="Number of pitches in the PA.<br>Click to see the pitch-by-pitch sequence." data-filter="1" data-name="Pit">Pit</th>
  <th data-stat="strikes_total" align="center"  class="tooltip"  tip="<strong>Strikes</strong><br>Includes both pitches in the zone and those swung at out of the zone." data-filter="1" data-name="Str">Str</th>
  <th data-stat="wpa_bat" align="center"  class="tooltip"  tip="<strong>Win Probability Added for Offensive Player</strong><br>Given average teams, this is the change in probability<br>caused by this batter during the game<br>A change of +/- 1 would indicate one win added or lost." data-filter="1" data-name="Win Probability Added (WPA)">WPA</th>
  <th data-stat="leverage_index_avg" align="center"  class="tooltip hide_non_quals"  tip="<strong>Average Leverage Index</strong><br>The average pressure the pitcher or batter saw in this game or season.<br>1.0 is average pressure, below 1.0 is low pressure and above 1.0 is high pressure." data-filter="1" data-name="aLI">aLI</th>
  <th data-stat="wpa_bat_pos" align="center"  class="tooltip"  tip="<strong>Win Probability Added</strong><br>Sum of positive events for this batter." data-filter="1" data-name="WPA+">WPA+</th>

Add 1 point for each out recorded, so 3 points for every complete inning pitched.<br>   3. Add 2 points for each inning completed after the 4th.<br>   4. Add 1 point for each strikeout.<br>   5. Subtract 2 points for each hit allowed.<br>   6. Subtract 4 points for each earned run allowed.<br>   7. Subtract 2 points for each unearned run allowed.<br>   8. Subtract 1 point for each walk.<br>" data-filter="1" data-name="GSc">GSc</th>

<P><a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.retrosheet.org/boxesetc/2012/B08250BOS2012.htm">Retrosheet.org Boxscore:BOS201208250</a>
<br><a rel="nofollow" href="http://backtobaseball.com/playballregularseason.php?page=0&IDindex=BOS201208250">BackToBaseball.com Game Playback</a>
<a name='explain'>
<div class="table_heading"><h3>Play-by-Play Explanation</h3></a></div>
<div id="pbpexplain" class="small_text" style="list-style-type: none">

<UL style="list-style-type: none;">

<LI><strong>Score</strong>- The score from the perspective of the batting team.</li>

<LI><strong>RoB</strong>- This gives the baserunner (Runners on Base)
configuration at the start of the play. "1-3" would mean runners on
first and third.  Clicking on this will show the defensive players and
baserunners on the field for this play.  </LI>

<LI><strong>Pit</strong>- When available, the number of pitches in this plate
appearance. Clicking on this number will show the sequence of pitches
thrown including, when available, things like runner going, ball
blocked, attempted pickoffs and the like.  We believe this data to be
as accurate as humanly possible, but there are going to be some errors
in the data, so please take it with a grain of salt. Clicking on this
will show the defensive players and baserunners on the field for this
play.  </LI>

<LI><strong>R/O</strong>- This has a "O" for every out on the play and an
"R" for every run that scored on the play.  Some plays will have both
in no particular order. </LI>


<LI><strong>Batter</strong>- The batter at the plate when this play occurred. If
the play is a baserunning event, then the batter's name will be
repeated as indicated by quotes.</LI>

<LI><strong>Pitcher</strong>- The pitcher on the mound when this play
occurred. </LI>

<LI><strong>wWPA</strong>- Winning Team's Win Probability Added.  The
amount that this play increased or decreased the eventual winning
team's probability of winning the game. <a
href="/about/wpa.shtml">More About Win Probability Added</a></li>

<LI><strong>wWE</strong>- Winning Team's Win Expectancy.  The
probability of the eventual winning team winning the game at the end of 
this play given two average teams playing each other. <a
href="/about/wpa.shtml">More About Win Probability Added</a></li>



<LI><strong>Play Detail</strong>- This is an explanation of the play that
occurred.  In some cases, batted ball location and type will be
indicated within parentheses.  Again, these are best efforts to the
record the game as it happened.  Also, plays made on the baserunners
(including the batter as a baserunner) will be indicated in
parentheses after the baserunner's name.  Advancement of baserunners
is given in cases where the advancement is not easily deduced or
obvious from the play.  For example, advancement for a walk will not
be given, but for a single or double it will be given.</LI> </UL>

<P>Please <a href="http://www.sports-reference.com/feedback/">report any
issues</a> or strangeness you see with the description of plays given
above.  We have tested several hundred different types of plays, but,
in all likelihood, there are still some errors or misinterpretations
of the play-by-play data.

</div>
 <p><div class="blockquote small_text italic_text clear_both">
The play-by-play information both shown and used to create certain
data sets was obtained free of charge from and is copyrighted by <a
rel="nofollow" href="http://www.retrosheet.org/">RetroSheet</a>.
</div>
</p>


<div class="blockquote small-text">
<p>In some cases, the results from play-by-play data will contradict
results in the official record.  The official record has many, many
errors, but we have not undertaken to reconcile those errors.
Pitch-by-pitch data should not be taken as completely accurate, though
we believe it to be as accurate as is currently possible.</p>

<p>Box scores and play-by-play outputs produced by Sports Reference LLC.  All Rights Reserved.</p>
</div>

 else if (element.attachEvent) element.attachEvent('on' + type, callback);
